<div class="sourceCode" id="cb1"><pre
class="sourceCode python"><code class="sourceCode python"><span id="cb1-1"><a href="#cb1-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co"># 准备好需要的包</span></span>
<span id="cb1-2"><a href="#cb1-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="im">import</span> re</span>
<span id="cb1-3"><a href="#cb1-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="im">import</span> json</span>
<span id="cb1-4"><a href="#cb1-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="im">import</span> time</span>
<span id="cb1-5"><a href="#cb1-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="im">import</span> requests</span>
<span id="cb1-6"><a href="#cb1-6" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb1-7"><a href="#cb1-7" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co"># 循环遍历分页内容</span></span>
<span id="cb1-8"><a href="#cb1-8" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="cf">for</span> page <span class="kw">in</span> <span class="bu">range</span>(<span class="dv">1</span>,<span class="dv">10</span>):</span>
<span id="cb1-9"><a href="#cb1-9" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="cf">try</span>:</span>
<span id="cb1-10"><a href="#cb1-10" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        <span class="co"># 目标</span></span>
<span id="cb1-11"><a href="#cb1-11" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        url<span class="op">=</span><span class="ss">f&quot;https://www.guo68.com/market?page=</span><span class="sc">{</span>page<span class="sc">}</span><span class="ss">&quot;</span></span>
<span id="cb1-12"><a href="#cb1-12" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        <span class="co"># action</span></span>
<span id="cb1-13"><a href="#cb1-13" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        response<span class="op">=</span>requests.get(url)</span>
<span id="cb1-14"><a href="#cb1-14" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb1-15"><a href="#cb1-15" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        <span class="bu">print</span>(response.text)</span>
<span id="cb1-16"><a href="#cb1-16" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        <span class="co"># 获取标签里的内容</span></span>
<span id="cb1-17"><a href="#cb1-17" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        a<span class="op">=</span>re.findall(<span class="st">&#39;&lt;li class=&quot;list1&quot;&gt;(.*?)&lt;/li&gt;&#39;</span>,response.text)[<span class="dv">1</span>:]</span>
<span id="cb1-18"><a href="#cb1-18" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        b<span class="op">=</span>re.findall(<span class="st">&#39;&lt;li class=&quot;list2 ellipsis&quot;&gt;(.*?)&lt;/li&gt;&#39;</span>,response.text)</span>
<span id="cb1-19"><a href="#cb1-19" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        c<span class="op">=</span>re.findall(<span class="st">&#39;&lt;li class=&quot;list3&quot;&gt;(￥</span><span class="er">\</span><span class="st">d.*/斤)&lt;/li&gt;&#39;</span>,response.text)[<span class="dv">1</span>:]</span>
<span id="cb1-20"><a href="#cb1-20" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        d<span class="op">=</span>re.findall(<span class="st">&#39;&lt;li class=&quot;list6&quot;&gt;(.*?)&lt;/li&gt;&#39;</span>,response.text)[<span class="dv">1</span>:]</span>
<span id="cb1-21"><a href="#cb1-21" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb1-22"><a href="#cb1-22" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        <span class="bu">print</span>(a,b,c,d)</span>
<span id="cb1-23"><a href="#cb1-23" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        <span class="co"># 对数据进行筛选，写入json文件</span></span>
<span id="cb1-24"><a href="#cb1-24" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        <span class="cf">for</span> name,city,price,date <span class="kw">in</span> <span class="bu">zip</span>(a,b,c,d):</span>
<span id="cb1-25"><a href="#cb1-25" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>            <span class="bu">print</span>(name,city,price,date)</span>
<span id="cb1-26"><a href="#cb1-26" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>            <span class="cf">if</span> name<span class="op">==</span><span class="st">&quot;其他&quot;</span>:</span>
<span id="cb1-27"><a href="#cb1-27" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>                <span class="cf">continue</span></span>
<span id="cb1-28"><a href="#cb1-28" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>            data<span class="op">=</span>{<span class="st">&quot;name&quot;</span>:name,<span class="st">&quot;city&quot;</span>:city,<span class="st">&quot;price&quot;</span>:price,<span class="st">&quot;date&quot;</span>:date}</span>
<span id="cb1-29"><a href="#cb1-29" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>            <span class="cf">with</span> <span class="bu">open</span>(<span class="st">&quot;fruit.json&quot;</span>,<span class="st">&#39;a&#39;</span>,encoding<span class="op">=</span><span class="st">&quot;utf-8&quot;</span>)<span class="im">as</span> f:</span>
<span id="cb1-30"><a href="#cb1-30" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>                json.dump(data,f,ensure_ascii<span class="op">=</span><span class="va">False</span>,indent<span class="op">=</span><span class="dv">1</span>)</span>
<span id="cb1-31"><a href="#cb1-31" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        <span class="co"># 每次执行完等待时间</span></span>
<span id="cb1-32"><a href="#cb1-32" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        time.sleep(<span class="dv">3</span>)</span>
<span id="cb1-33"><a href="#cb1-33" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="cf">except</span>:</span>
<span id="cb1-34"><a href="#cb1-34" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        <span class="cf">continue</span></span></code></pre></div>
